    628  3142							; new packing format
    629  3142							; sokoban
    630  3142
    631  3142
    632  3142							;Level element	Character	ASCII Code
    633  3142							;Wall	#	0x23
    634  3142							;Player	@	0x40
    635  3142							;Player on goal square	+	0x2b
    636  3142							;Box	$	0x24
    637  3142							;Box on goal square	*	0x2a
    638  3142							;Goal square	.	0x2e
    639  3142							;Floor	(Space)	0x20 or underscore
    640  3142
    641  3142							;This level ("Claire", by Lee J Haywood):
    642  3142
    643  3142							;#######
    644  3142							;#.@ # #
    645  3142							;#$* $ #
    646  3142							;#   $ #
    647  3142							;# ..	#
    648  3142							;#  *	#
    649  3142							;#######
    650  3142							;runlength encoded looks like this:
    651  3142
    652  3142							;The rows of the level are separated by "|"s. There has been a discussion in the Yahoo Group about what character should represent an empty square in May 2006. Finally the hyphen has been elected to be the standard character for an empty square. Nevertheless, programs are encouraged to support both, hyphens and underscores.

    112  32a6							; into the gameMode variable.

    282  334e		       00 07	   .SCRL_START_RIGHT =	SCREEN_WIDTH-.SCRL_START_LEFT	; 7

    285  334e		       00 22	   .SCRL_RIGHT_BIT =	%00100010

    290  334e		       00 06	   .SCRL_START_DOWN =	SCREEN_LINES-.SCRL_START_UP	; 6
    291  334e		       00 06	   .SCRL_STOP_DOWN =	SCREEN_LINES-.SCRL_STOP_UP	; 5

    293  334e		       00 88	   .SCRL_DOWN_BIT =	%10001000

    296  334e							; *** horizontal scrolling (unoptimized version): ***
    297  334e
    298  334e							; check for enabling horizontal scrolling:
    299  334e		       a5 99		      lda	ManX	; 3
    300  3350		       38		      sec		; 2
    301  3351		       e5 96		      sbc	BoardScrollX	; 3
    302  3353		       a8		      tay		; 2	     for later use
    303  3354		       a9 11		      lda	#.SCRL_LEFT_BIT	; 2
    304  3356		       c0 03		      cpy	#.SCRL_START_LEFT	; 2	     <3?
    305  3358		       30 06		      bmi	.startXScroll	; 2/3	     yes, scroll left
    306  335a		       c0 07		      cpy	#.SCRL_START_RIGHT	; 2	     <8?
    307  335c		       30 08		      bmi	.skipStartXScroll	; 2/3	     no
    308  335e		       a9 22		      lda	#.SCRL_RIGHT_BIT	; 2 = 22    yes, scroll right
    309  3360				   .startXScroll
    310  3360		       29 03		      and	#.SCRL_X_BITS >> 4	; 2
    311  3362		       05 97		      ora	scrollBits	; 3
    312  3364		       85 97		      sta	scrollBits	; 3 =	8
    313  3366				   .skipStartXScroll
    314  3366
    315  3366							; do horizontal scrolling:
    316  3366		       a5 97		      lda	scrollBits	; 3
    317  3368		       29 03		      and	#.SCRL_X_BITS >> 4	; 2
    318  336a		       f0 23		      beq	.skipXScroll	; 2/3
    319  336c		       29 22		      and	#.SCRL_RIGHT_BIT	; 2
    320  336e		       d0 0c		      bne	.xScrollRight	; 2/3=11/12
    321  3370
    322  3370							; scroll left:
    323  3370		       a5 96		      lda	BoardScrollX	; 3	     already at left edge?
    324  3372		       f0 15		      beq	.stopXScroll	; 2
    325  3374		       c6 96		      dec	BoardScrollX	; 5
    326  3376		       c0 02		      cpy	#.SCRL_STOP_LEFT-1	; 2
    327  3378		       10 0f		      bpl	.stopXScroll	; 2/3=15
    328  337a		       30 13		      bmi	.skipXScroll	; 3
    329  337c							;---------------------------------------
    330  337c				   .xScrollRight
    331  337c		       a6 96		      ldx	BoardScrollX	; 3
    332  337e		       e8		      inx		; 2
    333  337f		       e4 93		      cpx	BoardEdge_Right	; 3	     already at right edge?
    334  3381		       10 06		      bpl	.stopXScroll	; 2/3
    335  3383		       86 96		      stx	BoardScrollX	; 3
    336  3385		       c0 08		      cpy	#.SCRL_STOP_RIGHT+1	; 2
    337  3387		       10 06		      bpl	.skipXScroll	; 2/3=17/18
    338  3389				   .stopXScroll
    339  3389		       a5 97		      lda	scrollBits	; 3
    340  338b		       29 fc		      and	#(~(.SCRL_X_BITS >> 4))	; 2
    341  338d		       85 97		      sta	scrollBits	; 3 =	8
    342  338f				   .skipXScroll
    343  338f							; worst case: 22 + 8 + 12 + 17 + 8 = 67

    349  3391		       38		      sec		; 2

    517  3414
    518  3414							;----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    519  3414							; handle pause button for 2600 and 7800
    520  3414
    521  3414							; Timings:  NOT including palette setting or platform detect
    522  3414							; 2600:     no button press:	 11 cycles
    523  3414							;	     with button press:  21 cycles
    524  3414							; 7800      no button press:	 16 cycles
    525  3414							;	     with button press:  21 cycles
    526  3414
    527  3414
    528  3414
    529  3414		       00 08	   BW_SWITCH  =	$08	; NOTE: Shares bit position with SWCHB COLOUR/B&W SWITCH
    530  3414
    531  3414		       24 80		      bit	gameMode
    532  3416		       50 0b		      bvc	.pause7800	; 7800 platform
    533  3418
    534  3418							; 2600 pause logic...
    535  3418
    536  3418		       ad 82 02 	      lda	SWCHB
    537  341b		       45 80		      eor	gameMode
    538  341d		       29 08		      and	#BW_SWITCH
    539  341f		       f0 17		      beq	.setPauseCol	; no different to original state = no pause change
    540  3421		       d0 0f		      bne	.buttonDown	; unconditional
    541  3423
    542  3423							; 7800 pause logic...
    543  3423
    544  3423							; When the button is pressed, we check if it's the FIRST time it's pressed.
    545  3423							; This FIRST time is indicated by the PFLAG7800 being clear.  If it's the first time, we toggle the pause
    546  3423							; flag (BIT6) AND we toggle the PFLAG7800 so continued button-down does nothing.  When the button is
    547  3423							; released, then we again toggle the PFLAG7800, allowing a FIRST time check once again, when the button
    548  3423							; is next pressed.
    549  3423
    550  3423		       a9 08	   .pause7800 lda	#BW_SWITCH
    551  3425		       2c 82 02 	      bit	SWCHB
    552  3428		       f0 04		      beq	.pausePress
    553  342a		       05 80		      ora	gameMode	; not pressed, so enable first time press
    554  342c		       d0 08		      bne	.fixPause	; unconditional
    555  342e
    556  342e		       24 80	   .pausePress bit	gameMode
    557  3430		       f0 06		      beq	.setPauseCol	; NOT the first time in pause - so do nothing new
    558  3432
    559  3432							; Button is down, and we have detected it as a FIRST-TIME button press.
    560  3432
    561  3432		       45 80	   .buttonDown eor	gameMode	; toggle first time flag(7800) or current switch state(2600)
    562  3434		       49 80		      eor	#GAMEMODE_PAUSED	; toggle pause flag
    563  3436		       85 80	   .fixPause  sta	gameMode
    564  3438
    565  3438		       a5 80	   .setPauseCol lda	gameMode	; are we paused?
    566  343a		       10 07		      bpl	.exitPause	; only show pause colour when actually paused
    567  343c
    568  343c		       a6 81		      ldx	Platform
    569  343e		       bd a9 f4 	      lda	pscol,x
    570  3441		       85 a9		      sta	BGColour	; set main screen background colour.  RED is paused.
    571  3443
    572  3443				   .exitPause
    573  3443
    574  3443							;----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    575  3443
    576  3443							; has to be done AFTER screen display, because it disables the effect!
    577  3443		       a5 82		      lda	rnd	; 3	 randomly reposition the Cosmic Ark missile
    578  3445		       85 62		      sta	HMM0	; 3	 this assumes that HMOVE is called at least once/frame
    579  3447
    580  3447							; "Flash" has highest BG colour priority
    581  3447
    582  3447		       a6 bc		      ldx	ColourTimer
    583  3449		       f0 06		      beq	noFlashBG
    584  344b		       c6 bc		      dec	ColourTimer
    585  344d		       a9 0e		      lda	#WHITE
    586  344f		       85 a9		      sta	BGColour
    587  3451				   noFlashBG
    588  3451
    589  3451							;		  lda extraLifeTimer
    590  3451							;		  beq alreadyBlack2
    591  3451							;		  dec extraLifeTimer
    592  3451							;alreadyBlack2
    593  3451
    594  3451							; Handle the player joystick reading. We do it *every frame* so that we can incorporate a two-frame
    595  3451							; buffer.  This is designed to give a little better responsiveness to the 'quick tap' movement.
    596  3451
    597  3451		       a5 90		      lda	BufferedJoystick	; previous frame
    598  3453		       85 91		      sta	BufferedJoystick+1	; -> buffered
    599  3455
    600  3455							; Create a 'standardised' joystick with D4-D7 having bits CLEAR if the appropriate direction is chosen.
    601  3455							; P2 is shifted UP, so we don't need to worry in usage elsewhere (it's same format as a P1 joystick)
    602  3455
    603  3455		       a5 98		      lda	whichPlayer	; 3
    604  3457		       25 a6		      and	jtoggle	; 3
    605  3459		       aa		      tax		; 2
    606  345a
    607  345a		       b5 4c		      lda	INPT4,x	; 4
    608  345c		       85 92		      sta	BufferedButton	; 3 = 15
    609  345e
    610  345e		       ad 80 02 	      lda	SWCHA	; 4
    611  3461
    612  3461		       ca		      dex		; 2
    613  3462		       30 04		      bmi	notP2	; 2/3= 8/9
    614  3464
    615  3464		       0a		      asl		; 2
    616  3465		       0a		      asl		; 2
    617  3466		       0a		      asl		; 2
    618  3467		       0a		      asl		; 2 =	8
    619  3468		       85 90	   notP2      sta	BufferedJoystick	; 3
    620  346a
    621  346a
    622  346a							; "Scoring timer" reset stomp comment
    623  346a
    624  346a		       a5 be		      lda	scoringTimer

    626  346e		       c6 be		      dec	scoringTimer
    627  3470		       d0 06		      bne	timer0now
    628  3472		       a5 bf		      lda	scoringFlags
    629  3474		       29 fc		      and	#<(~DISPLAY_FLAGS)	;	 switches to time display
    630  3476		       85 bf		      sta	scoringFlags
    631  3478				   timer0now
    632  3478
    633  3478							; fall through
    634  3478
    635  3478							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    636  3478							; Player animation happens *every* frame so that we get good animation speeds.  Note that
    637  3478							; the player animation consists of running a small animation 'program', and then actually drawing
    638  3478							; the player.	The draw is the neat bit, because all it does is update some self-modifying pointers
    639  3478							; inside the actual draw kernel in the appropriate bank.
    640  3478
    641  3478
      0  3478					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	AnimatePlayers	; in GENERIC_BANK_1
      1  3478		       00 06	   BANK_AnimatePlayers =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3478					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3478				   AnimatePlayers
    643  3478
    644  3478							; Optimised 7/1/2012 -- single page tables
    645  3478
    646  3478							; This interesting code performs the animations for the player(s) and sets the
    647  3478							; pointers INSIDE the row bank for the draw code to point to the correct player
    648  3478							; shape.  Kind of neat, as it doesn't require any shape copying (=speed!)
    649  3478
    650  3478
    651  3478							; Cycle the player through his animation list.  The animation of a player is a direct
    652  3478							; pointer to the actual shape used to display the player.  This shape is in turn
    653  3478							; written to the current bank's self-modifying locations for the draw.  Since
    654  3478							; we are effectively drawing from this current bank, the same code can be used
    655  3478							; to 'undraw' the player as required.
    656  3478
    657  3478
    658  3478							; x = player index
    659  3478							; sets ManAnimation = FRAME to display for player
    660  3478							; ManAnimation = index of player program into Manimate list
    661  3478
    662  3478		       24 80		      bit	gameMode
    663  347a		       30 2c		      bmi	AnimationOK	; don't animate during pause
    664  347c
    665  347c		       c6 9e		      dec	ManDelayCount
    666  347e		       10 28		      bpl	AnimationOK
    667  3480
    668  3480		       a4 9f	   ReloadAnimation ldy	ManAnimation
    669  3482		       b9 00 f6    ContinueAnim lda	Manimate,y	; delay count
    670  3485		       d0 07		      bne	NewFrameOK
    671  3487		       b9 01 f6 	      lda	Manimate+1,y
    672  348a		       a8		      tay
    673  348b		       4c 82 f4 	      jmp	ContinueAnim
    674  348e
    675  348e		       10 0d	   NewFrameOK bpl	doDelay
    676  3490
    677  3490		       c8		      iny		; handle a REFLECT
    678  3491		       a5 a2		      lda	ManLastDirection
    679  3493		       29 f7		      and	#%11110111
    680  3495		       19 00 f6 	      ora	Manimate,y
    681  3498		       85 a2		      sta	ManLastDirection
    682  349a
    683  349a		       c8		      iny
    684  349b		       d0 e5		      bne	ContinueAnim
    685  349d
    686  349d		       85 9e	   doDelay    sta	ManDelayCount
    687  349f
    688  349f		       c8		      iny
    689  34a0		       b9 00 f6 	      lda	Manimate,y
    690  34a3		       85 a1		      sta	ManAnimationFrameLO
    691  34a5
    692  34a5		       c8		      iny
    693  34a6		       84 9f		      sty	ManAnimation
    694  34a8
    695  34a8		       60	   AnimationOK rts
    696  34a9
    697  34a9
    698  34a9
    699  34a9		       40 40	   pscol      .byte.b	$40, $40
    700  34ab		       60 60		      .byte.b	$60, $60
    701  34ad

------- FILE i2c_v2.2.inc LEVEL 3 PASS 3
      0  34ad					      include	"i2c_v2.2.inc"
      1  34ad							;
      2  34ad							; i2c_v2.2.inc
      3  34ad							;
      4  34ad							;
      5  34ad							; AtariVox EEPROM Driver
      6  34ad							;
      7  34ad							; By Alex Herbert, 2004
      8  34ad							;
      9  34ad							; Optimisations by Thomas Jentzsch, 2006/2008
     10  34ad							;
     11  34ad
     12  34ad
     13  34ad							; I/O Constants
     14  34ad
     15  34ad		       00 04	   I2C_SDA_MASK equ	$04
     16  34ad		       00 08	   I2C_SCL_MASK equ	$08
     17  34ad
     18  34ad
     19  34ad							; Signalling Macros
     20  34ad
     21  34ad							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_0
     22  34ad							;    lda     #$00
     23  34ad							;    sta     SWCHA
     24  34ad							;  ENDM
     25  34ad
     26  34ad							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_1
     27  34ad							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     28  34ad							;    sta     SWCHA
     29  34ad							;  ENDM
     30  34ad
     31  34ad							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_IN
     32  34ad							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     33  34ad							;    sta     SWACNT
     34  34ad							;  ENDM
     35  34ad
     36  34ad							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_OUT
     37  34ad							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     38  34ad							;    sta     SWACNT
     39  34ad							;  ENDM
     40  34ad
     41  34ad
     42  34ad					      MAC	i2c_start
     43  34ad							; I2C_SCL_1
     44  34ad					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)*2	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     45  34ad					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     46  34ad							; I2C_SDA_OUT
     47  34ad					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     48  34ad					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     49  34ad							; total: 12 cycles
     50  34ad					      ENDM
     51  34ad
     52  34ad
     53  34ad					      MAC	i2c_txbit
     54  34ad							; I2C_SCL_0
     55  34ad					      lda	#%0011	; 2
     56  34ad					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     57  34ad							; set bit
     58  34ad					      adc	#%1000	; 2
     59  34ad					      sta	SWACNT	; 4	     SDA = !C (a = %1000 / %1100)
     60  34ad							; I2C_SCL_1
     61  34ad					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK	; 2
     62  34ad					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     63  34ad							; total: 18 cycles
     64  34ad					      ENDM
     65  34ad
     66  34ad
     67  34ad					      MAC	i2c_txnack
     68  34ad							; I2C_SCL_0
     69  34ad					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK*2	; 2	     $00
     70  34ad					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     71  34ad							; I2C_SDA_IN
     72  34ad					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     73  34ad					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     74  34ad							; I2C_SCL_1
     75  34ad					      nop		; 2	     required for timing!
     76  34ad					      sta	SWCHA	; 4	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     77  34ad							; total: 18 cycles
     78  34ad					      ENDM
     79  34ad
     80  34ad
     81  34ad							; Subroutine Macros
     82  34ad
     83  34ad					      MAC	i2c_subs
     84  34ad
     85  34ad				   i2c_startread
     86  34ad							; use V to flag if previous byte needs ACK
     87  34ad					      ldy	#%10100001	; 2	     eeprom read command
     88  34ad					      .byte	$2c	; 2
     89  34ad				   i2c_startwrite
     90  34ad					      ldy	#%10100000	; 2	     eeprom write command
     91  34ad					      I2C_START		;12	     start signal (clears V flag)
     92  34ad					      tya		; 2 = 16
     93  34ad				   i2c_txbyte
     94  34ad					      eor	#$ff	; 2	     invert data byte
     95  34ad					      sec		; 2
     96  34ad					      rol		; 2 =	6    shift loop bit into a
     97  34ad				   i2c_txbyteloop
     98  34ad					      tay		; 2
     99  34ad					      I2C_TXBIT		;18	     transmit
    100  34ad					      tya		; 2
    101  34ad					      asl		; 2	     shift next bit into C
    102  34ad					      bne	i2c_txbyteloop	; 2= 26/27
    103  34ad
    104  34ad							; receive acknowledge bit
    105  34ad
    106  34ad					      beq	i2c_rxbit	;43 = 43
    107  34ad							; i2c_txbyte: 264 cycles
    108  34ad							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    109  34ad
    110  34ad				   i2c_rxbyte
    111  34ad					      bvc	i2c_rxskipack	; 2	     previous byte needs acknowledge?
    112  34ad					      jsr	i2c_txack	;24	     transmit acknowledge bit
    113  34ad
    114  34ad				   i2c_rxskipack
    115  34ad					      bit	i2c_rxbyte	; 4	     set V - next byte(s) require acknowledge
    116  34ad
    117  34ad					      lda	#1	; 2
    118  34ad				   i2c_rxbyteloop
    119  34ad					      tay		; 2 =	2
    120  34ad				   i2c_rxbit		;	     receive bit in C
    121  34ad					      I2C_TXNACK		;18 = 18
    122  34ad
    123  34ad					      lda	SWCHA	; 4
    124  34ad					      lsr		; 2
    125  34ad					      lsr		; 2
    126  34ad					      lsr		; 2 = 10    C = SDA
    127  34ad
    128  34ad					      tya		; 2
    129  34ad					      rol		; 2	     rotate into Y
    130  34ad					      bcc	i2c_rxbyteloop	; 2=	6/7
    131  34ad
    132  34ad							; received byte in A
    133  34ad					      rts		; 6 =	6
    134  34ad							; i2c_rxbit:  40 cycles
    135  34ad							; i2c_rxbyte: 310/333 cycles
    136  34ad							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    137  34ad
    138  34ad				   i2c_stopread
    139  34ad					      bvc	i2c_stopwrite	; 2
    140  34ad					      ldy	#$80	; 2
    141  34ad					      jsr	i2c_rxbit	;46	     transmit no-acknowledge
    142  34ad
    143  34ad				   i2c_stopwrite
    144  34ad					      jsr	i2c_txack	;30
    145  34ad
    146  34ad							; return port to input mode
    147  34ad					      lda	#0	; 2	     0
    148  34ad					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    149  34ad					      rts		; 6 = 12
    150  34ad							; i2c_stopread:  45/92
    151  34ad							; i2c_stopwrite: 42
    152  34ad							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  34ad
    154  34ad				   i2c_txack
    155  34ad							; I2C_SCL_0
    156  34ad					      lda	#0	; 2	     $00
    157  34ad					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    158  34ad							; I2C_SDA_OUT
    159  34ad					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
    160  34ad					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    161  34ad							; I2C_SCL_1
    162  34ad					      asl		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
    163  34ad					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    164  34ad
    165  34ad					      rts		; 6
    166  34ad							; total: 24 cycles
    167  34ad							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    168  34ad
    169  34ad					      ENDM
    170  34ad
    171  34ad
    172  34ad

      0  3518					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	ReadSaveKey	; = 2371

    757  352d		       20 d6 f4 	      jsr	i2c_rxbyte	;6+333      read byte from EEPROM
    758  3530		       c9 ff		      cmp	#$ff	; 2	     EEPROM slot empty?
    759  3532		       d0 02		      bne	.skipEmpty	; 2/3	      no, skip clear
    760  3534		       a9 00		      lda	#0	; 2	     clear EEPROM slot
    761  3536				   .skipEmpty
    762  3536		       95 d5		      sta	highScoreSK,x	; 4
    763  3538		       ca		      dex		; 2
    764  3539		       10 f2		      bpl	.loopRead	; 2/3= 354
    765  353b
    766  353b							; stop read:
    767  353b		       4c f9 f4 	      jmp	i2c_stopread	;3+92=95    terminate read
    768  353e
    769  353e							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      0  353e					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	WriteSaveKey	; = 1751
      1  353e		       00 06	   BANK_WriteSaveKey =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  353e					      SUBROUTINE
      3  353e				   WriteSaveKey
    771  353e
    772  353e							; check if new high score:
    773  353e		       a6 d5		      ldx	highScoreSK	; 3
    774  3540		       e8		      inx		; 2
    775  3541		       f0 34		      beq	NoSKfound	; 2/3	     no new high score, abort
    776  3543
    777  3543							; setup SaveKey:
    778  3543		       a5 d8		      lda	startCave	; 3	     load start cave*5 and level
    779  3545		       a6 d9		      ldx	startLevel	; 3
    780  3547		       20 59 f5 	      jsr	SetupSaveKey	; 6+853
    781  354a		       90 2b		      bcc	NoSKfound	; 2/3
    782  354c
    783  354c							;    lda     #$64
    784  354c							;    sta     COLUBK
    785  354c
    786  354c							; write high score:
    787  354c		       a2 02		      ldx	#3-1	; 2 = 841
    788  354e				   .loopWrite
    789  354e		       b5 d5		      lda	highScoreSK,x	; 4
    790  3550		       20 bc f4 	      jsr	i2c_txbyte	;6+264      transmit to EEPROM
    791  3553		       ca		      dex		; 2
    792  3554		       10 f8		      bpl	.loopWrite	; 2/3= 837
    793  3556
    794  3556							; stop write:
    795  3556		       4c 00 f5 	      jmp	i2c_stopwrite	; 3+42= 45  terminate write and commit to memory
    796  3559
    797  3559
    798  3559							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      0  3559					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SetupSaveKey	; = 853
      1  3559		       00 06	   BANK_SetupSaveKey =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3559					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3559				   SetupSaveKey
    800  3559
    801  3559							; calculate slot;
    802  3559							; a = cave (5*n): A=$00; E=$05; I=$0a; M=$0f
    803  3559							; x = level (0..4)
    804  3559		       85 da		      sta	offsetSK	; 3
    805  355b		       8a		      txa		; 2
    806  355c		       18		      clc		; 2
    807  355d		       65 da		      adc	offsetSK	; 3
    808  355f		       85 da		      sta	offsetSK	; 3
    809  3561		       0a		      asl		; 2	     multiply by 3
    810  3562		       65 da		      adc	offsetSK	; 3
    811  3564		       69 00		      adc	#<SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2
    812  3566		       aa		      tax		; 2 = 22
    813  3567							; detect SaveKey:
    814  3567		       20 b0 f4 	      jsr	i2c_startwrite	;6+280
    815  356a		       d0 0a		      bne	.exitSK	; 2/3
    816  356c
    817  356c							; setup address:
    818  356c		       b8		      clv		; 2
    819  356d		       a9 06		      lda	#>SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2	     upper byte of address
    820  356f		       20 bc f4 	      jsr	i2c_txbyte	;6+264
    821  3572		       8a		      txa		; 2	     x = lower byte offset
    822  3573		       4c bc f4 	      jmp	i2c_txbyte	;3+264      returns C==1
    823  3576
    824  3576				   .exitSK
    825  3576		       18		      clc
    826  3577				   NoSKfound
    827  3577		       60		      rts
    828  3577					      ENDIF

      0  3845					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	CopyROMShadowToRAM	; in INITBANK
      1  3845		       00 07	   BANK_CopyROMShadowToRAM =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3845					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3845				   CopyROMShadowToRAM
     84  3845
     85  3845							; Function copies a RAM prototype ROM bank into the destination RAM bank.  Typically
     86  3845							; the variable definitions are in the ROM shadow because this allows auto-initialisation
     87  3845							; of the variable contents from ROM declarations, but still allows access to them as
     88  3845							; variables when the correct RAM bank is switched in.	Code is also, of course, copied
     89  3845							; into the RAM destination so that code is callable whenever the ROM *or* RAM bank is
     90  3845							; switched in.  Further, if multiple copies are made to multiple RAM banks, then the
     91  3845							; code co-lives in all banks and may run even as bankswitching occurs between those
     92  3845							; banks -- by the very code itself.
     93  3845
     94  3845							; Note: Relies on ROM_Bank having being set via CALL mechanism to call this function
     95  3845		       85 b7		      sta	Board_AddressR+1
     96  3847		       86 d3		      stx	O_ROM_Source_Bank	; source bank
     97  3849		       84 bb		      sty	RAM_Bank	; destination bank
     98  384b
     99  384b		       a0 00		      ldy	#0
    100  384d		       84 b6		      sty	Board_AddressR
    101  384f		       84 b8		      sty	Board_AddressW
    102  3851		       a9 14		      lda	#>($1000+RAM_WRITE)
    103  3853		       85 b9		      sta	Board_AddressW+1
    104  3855
    105  3855							; Iterate 4 pages (1K) for complete bank copy
    106  3855
    107  3855		       a9 04		      lda	#4
    108  3857		       85 d2		      sta	O_CopyCount
    109  3859
    110  3859		       84 d4	   CopyPage   sty	O_Index
    111  385b		       a5 d3		      lda	O_ROM_Source_Bank
    112  385d		       20 32 f8 	      jsr	GetROMByte	; get byte from ROM shadow bank
    113  3860							;tax
    114  3860		       a4 d4		      ldy	O_Index
    115  3862		       a6 bb		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    116  3864		       20 40 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 write byte to RAM bank
    117  3867
    118  3867		       a4 d4		      ldy	O_Index
    119  3869		       c8		      iny
    120  386a		       d0 ed		      bne	CopyPage
    121  386c
    122  386c		       e6 b7		      inc	Board_AddressR+1
    123  386e		       e6 b9		      inc	Board_AddressW+1
    124  3870
    125  3870		       c6 d2		      dec	O_CopyCount
    126  3872		       d0 e5		      bne	CopyPage
    127  3874
    128  3874		       a4 bb		      ldy	RAM_Bank	; TODO: remove!?
    129  3876		       60		      rts
    130  3877
    131  3877
    132  3877							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      0  3877					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SetPlatformColours	; in INITBANK

      3  3877				   SetPlatformColours
    134  3877
    135  3877							; Now modify the hardwired colours so that we're correctly switched for NTSC/PAL
    136  3877							; The platform (0=NTSC, 1=PAL) is set from the right difficulty switch
    137  3877							; Note: This relies on DrawTheScreen starting on page boundary so that the (),y
    138  3877							; addressing will not violate the page-crossing restriction of 3E.
    139  3877

    153  3883		       d0 07		      bne	.skipPatch

    156  3889		       20 40 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 set index/rts
    157  388c				   .skipPatch
    158  388c
    159  388c		       a2 02		      ldx	#3-1
    160  388e				   .loopColor
    161  388e		       86 d2		      stx	colorIdx
    162  3890							; set PF colors

    164  3892		       bc b7 f0 	      ldy	SelfModColOfsTbl,x
    165  3895							;tax
    166  3895		       a6 bb		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    167  3897		       20 40 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 copy PF colour RED/GREEN/BLUE to self-modifying RAM
    168  389a							; set player colors
    169  389a		       a6 d2		      ldx	colorIdx
    170  389c		       bd ba f0 	      lda	SelfModePlayerTbl,x
    171  389f		       a4 81		      ldy	Platform
    172  38a1		       c0 02		      cpy	#PAL
    173  38a3		       90 02		      bcc	.platform0

    175  38a7				   .platform0

    177  38aa							;tax
    178  38aa		       a6 bb		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    179  38ac		       20 40 f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 copy player colour RED/GREEN/BLUE to self-modifying RAM
    180  38af							; loop
    181  38af		       a6 d2		      ldx	colorIdx
    182  38b1		       ca		      dex
    183  38b2		       10 da		      bpl	.loopColor
    184  38b4
    185  38b4		       a4 bb		      ldy	RAM_Bank
    186  38b6		       60		      rts

      0  78b6					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SwitchObjects	;=72
      1  78b6		       00 0f	   BANK_SwitchObjects =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  78b6					      SUBROUTINE
      3  78b6				   SwitchObjects
    192  78b6							; TJ: used by:
    193  78b6							; - BANK_FIXED.asm
    194  78b6
    195  78b6							; The game loop has come to an end. The only possible "still happening" thing is the sort, which runs
    196  78b6							; in parallel with other processes (objects, draw stack, etc). We may or may not want to wait for the
    197  78b6							; sort to complete.  This code does all the checks needed to switch to the next game frame.
    198  78b6
    199  78b6		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    200  78b9		       c9 03		      cmp	#SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS	; 2
    201  78bb		       90 f8		      bcc	EarlyAbort	; 2/3= 8
      0  78bd					      STRESS_TIME	SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS
      1  78bd				  -	      IF	TEST_SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS = 1
      2  78bd				  -
      3  78bd				  -
      4  78bd				  -
      5  78bd				  -
      6  78bd				  -
      7  78bd				  -	      echo	"***** WARNING! STRESS_TIME enabled @", ., "! *****"
      8  78bd				  -	      bne	. - 7
      9  78bd					      ENDIF
    203  78bd
    204  78bd							; If we're undertime, then abort. The sort will continue to run, and that's great. Only when
    205  78bd							; we're at the throttle cutoff do we switch game-frames.
    206  78bd
    207  78bd							;sec
    208  78bd		       a5 ad		      lda	Throttle	;3
    209  78bf		       e9 a0		      sbc	#MAX_THROTTLE	;2
    210  78c1		       90 f2		      bcc	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 plenty of time left!
    211  78c3
    212  78c3							; Time is up. But we may be in a level which requires perfect sorting
    213  78c3							; So we check for these levels, and wait for the sort to complete for those.
    214  78c3
    215  78c3		       24 ac		      bit	levelDisplay	;3
    216  78c5		       50 08		      bvc	keepFractional	;2/3		 screen does not require complete sort
    217  78c7
    218  78c7							; We have a level which requires the sort to go to completion
    219  78c7							; Check to see if the sort is finished...
    220  78c7
    221  78c7		       a4 c8		      ldy	sortPtr	;3
    222  78c9		       d0 ea		      bne	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    223  78cb		       a4 c7		      ldy	sortRequired	;3
    224  78cd		       10 e6		      bpl	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    225  78cf
    226  78cf		       85 ad	   keepFractional sta	Throttle	;3		 save fractional 'left over' bit
    227  78d1
    228  78d1							; Pause the game with B/W switch:
    229  78d1
    230  78d1		       a5 80		      lda	gameMode
    231  78d3							;		  ora LookingAround		  ; New behavour of looking around pauses creatures when activated.
    232  78d3		       30 14		      bmi	.paused	; pause flag set
    233  78d5
    234  78d5							; Now that we have completed processing the object stack, we switch
    235  78d5							; the stack bank pointers for the next time around.
    236  78d5
    237  78d5		       a5 85		      lda	ObjStackNum	;3
    238  78d7		       49 01		      eor	#1	;2
    239  78d9		       aa		      tax		;2
    240  78da		       86 85		      stx	ObjStackNum	;3		 swap stacks @here
    241  78dc
    242  78dc							; STOP the sort so it doesn't corrupt the "other" object stack. Sort may get a look-in immediately after
    243  78dc							; this code is finished, so we don't want it to do something unexpected!
    244  78dc
    245  78dc		       a0 ff		      ldy	#<(-1)	;2
    246  78de		       84 c7		      sty	sortRequired	;3
    247  78e0		       c8		      iny		;2		 Y==0
    248  78e1		       84 c8		      sty	sortPtr	;3
    249  78e3
    250  78e3							; Initialise the iterator and stack pointer for next time around.
    251  78e3							; Previously the stack pointer auto-initialised by popping the stack. Now we have an iterator it's
    252  78e3							; necessary to initialise both.
    253  78e3
    254  78e3		       84 d0		      sty	ObjIterator	;3		 Y==0
    255  78e5		       94 86		      sty	ObjStackPtr,x	;4
    256  78e7
    257  78e7		       84 89		      sty	ScreenDrawPhase	;3
    258  78e9				   .paused
    259  78e9		       60	   quickExit  rts		;6
    260  78ea

    318  792d
    319  792d							; IF the creature runs out of time to do stuff, then rts HOWEVER the creature must eventually do something
    320  792d							;  as it will be continually called in available time-slices until it does. This can lockup the system.

    367  795a							; Objects are unceremoniously dumped when there's not enough space.  This is just trying to cater

      0  79f4					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	TimeSlice
      1  79f4		       00 0f	   BANK_TimeSlice =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  79f4					      SUBROUTINE
      3  79f4				   TimeSlice
    553  79f4
    554  79f4							; FIRST check the time is sufficient for the smallest of the timeslices. Not much point
    555  79f4							; going ahead if there's insufficient time. This allows the previous character drawing to
    556  79f4							; be much smaller in time, as they don't have to include the timeslice code overhead.
    557  79f4
    558  79f4		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    559  79f7		       c9 05		      cmp	#SEGTIME_MINIMUM_TIMESLICE	; 2
    560  79f9		       90 de		      bcc	timeExit	; 2(3)
    561  79fb
    562  79fb							; Uses the phase variable to vector to the correct processing code for the given timeslice
    563  79fb							; Code may be in any bank. Avoid the fixed bank at all costs!	Once a section is complete
    564  79fb							; it should increment ScreenDrawPhase.
    565  79fb
    566  79fb							; Switched-in bank(s) are undefined after this function is called!
    567  79fb
    568  79fb		       a9 06		      lda	#BANK_TS_PhaseVectorLO	; 2
    569  79fd		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3
    570  79ff
    571  79ff		       a6 89		      ldx	ScreenDrawPhase	; 3		 current phase of drawing
    572  7a01		       bd d1 f3 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorLO,x	; 4
    573  7a04		       85 d2		      sta	TS_Vector	; 3
    574  7a06		       bd d6 f3 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorHI,x	; 4
    575  7a09		       85 d3		      sta	TS_Vector+1	; 3
    576  7a0b
    577  7a0b		       bd db f3 	      lda	TS_PhaseBank,x	; 4
    578  7a0e		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3		 switch bank
    579  7a10
    580  7a10		       6c d2 00 	      jmp	(TS_Vector)	; 3 = 40	 vector to timeslice handler
    581  7a13
    582  7a13							; = 55 minimum return time (if segtime abort)

    813  7ae6							; the (at least) 220 cycles wasted in the above... bugs me!
    814  7ae6							; the below is an unrolled version.  I've moved some other code between the sync writes, effectively saving um... 22 cycles/frame.
    815  7ae6							; This required TIM64T values to be increased by 1 for each platform (we have actually gained back some usable time :)
    816  7ae6
    817  7ae6							;bit NextLevelTrigger
    818  7ae6							;bpl NextCaveLevel		  ; game-triggered next level

    821  7ae6							; Note: VSYNC must NOT be on when starting a new cave! Else you get annoying TV signals.
    822  7ae6
    823  7ae6		       a9 0e		      lda	#%1110	; VSYNC ON
    824  7ae8		       85 42	   .loopVSync sta	WSYNC
    825  7aea		       85 40		      sta	VSYNC
    826  7aec		       4a		      lsr
    827  7aed		       d0 f9		      bne	.loopVSync	; branch until VYSNC has been reset
    828  7aef
    829  7aef							; moved *after* the loop since this allows to *increase* timer values by 1!

    853  7b08							; A 42-cycle timing window in the screen draw code.  Perform any general
    854  7b08							; per-frame code here, provided it takes exactly 42 cycles to execute.

      2  7b0a
      3  7b0a				  -	      IF	.CYCLES < 2
      4  7b0a				  -	      ECHO	"MACRO ERROR: 'SLEEP': Duration must be > 1"

      6  7b0a					      ENDIF

      9  7b0a					      IFNCONST	NO_ILLEGAL_OPCODES
     10  7b0a		       04 00		      nop	0
     11  7b0c				  -	      ELSE
     12  7b0c				  -	      bit	VSYNC
     13  7b0c					      ENDIF
     14  7b0c				   .CYCLES    SET	.CYCLES - 3
     15  7b0c					      ENDIF

     18  7b0c		       ea		      nop
     19  7b0d					      REPEND
